Therefore, you need to reflect on this, come to your peace with it and never, my golden queen, never request another such concession from me.” </i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1444057120ra/16446962.gif" width="500" height="279" alt="Drogo" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i> “You love the feel of me” </i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1444057120ra/16446963.gif" width="500" height="350" alt=" Drogo&amp;Daenerys" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>“You don’t have to have had something to want it or need it but when you have something you liked… very much… and it is taken away, and you want it back, it can become a hunger.” </i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1444057120ra/16446966.gif" width="310" height="254" alt=" Drogo&amp;Daenerys" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>"I gave up my world for you, Lahn. I even felt 'pride' that I could endure, that I could be a good queen to you.......Everything I did in this fucking place, even before I fell in love with you, was for...fucking...YOU." ” </i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1444057120ra/16446965.gif" width="396" height="254" alt="DrogoDaenerys" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <i> “Then I whispered, “I love you, my Lahn,” and heard the swift hiss of his intake of breath.               <span id="reviewTextContainer1438150615" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer14499730471049913886">I have read this wonderful book many many times. I can honestly say, that this is my absolute favorite KA book...and I have many KA favorits.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1489143555ra/22188847.gif' alt='YqiFWKK.gif (431×281)' width='219' height='143' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I never took the time to review this one though, because I love it so much...which is making it hard for me to write down a proper review. I have so many many feelings about this one, that I don't even know how or where to start.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1489143555ra/22188848.gif' alt='giphy.gif (500×262)' width='305' height='160' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Being that this is one of my all time favorite books though, I felt I had to write down something....so here goes.<br/><br/>Circe is a 35 ye</span>
  <span id="freeText14499730471049913886" style="display:none">I have read this wonderful book many many times. I can honestly say, that this is my absolute favorite KA book...and I have many KA favorits.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1489143555ra/22188847.gif" alt="YqiFWKK.gif (431×281)" width="219" height="143" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I never took the time to review this one though, because I love it so much...which is making it hard for me to write down a proper review. I have so many many feelings about this one, that I don't even know how or where to start.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1489143555ra/22188848.gif" alt="giphy.gif (500×262)" width="305" height="160" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Being that this is one of my all time favorite books though, I felt I had to write down something....so here goes.<br><br>Circe is a 35 year old woman from Seattle. She has a wonderful life. Her mother was murdered when she was 10, but she has a very loving father, who means the world to her. She has a good job working for his company and a lot of friends. She is single and a bit unlucky in love, but all in all she is very happy.....but that's all about to change.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1489143555ra/22188849.gif" alt="tumblr_n58dl5g6uz1s99nn5o1_500.gif (500×241)" width="309" height="149" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>One day she wakes up in a cage with a bunch of other women, in a world that is not her own. Everything is different. The people, the time,  the land, the language.... .......every...fucking....thing !!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1489143555ra/22188850.gif" alt="giphy.gif (499×281)" width="351" height="198" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Thankfully one of the women speaks her language and explains to her what is going on.  Apparently all the women are part of a ritual called "The Wife Hunt".  Korwahk tribe has this ritual every 2 years. All the women are paraded in front of the warrior men...set free to run...and are then hunted. Did I say hunted....why yes I did. This is how they capture their new wife. Once captured, they are claimed.....and with claimed I mean raped. Did I say raped....yes I most certainly did...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1489143555ra/22188851.gif" alt="13835182.gif (500×280)" width="355" height="199" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now Circe is fucked, not only because she woke up in a parralel universe and is about to be hunted and claimed. No she is also fucked because she has caught the eye of Dax Lahn, the King of the Korwahk Horde....and he is a savage. He is supposed to be a cold and heartless warrior and he is about to hunt her down.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1489143555ra/22188852.gif" alt="Are-you-fuckin-kidding-me-GIF.gif (245×235)" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Which is what he does. He hunts, captures and rapes her. I won't lie, it was hard to read. Circe is claimed and crowned "the golden queen" to her new warrior husband. Things don't get much easier. Circe does not speak the language, she can't make herself clear. So the violations keeps happening... He doesn't talk to her and just keeps taking...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1489143555ra/22188853.gif" alt="tumblr_nwdkr2qpbt1uen1r9o1_400.gif (400×263)" width="287" height="189" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>That's when Diandra comes in and things start to change. Diandra has been living with the Kohrwak tribe for a long time and is married to one of the warriors. She however speaks english and is to be Circe's  translator. Slowly communication becomes easier and Circe and Lahn start connecting. They become closer and closer and it was beautiful to read and see how much Lahn liked his new bride...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1489143555ra/22188854.gif" alt="2c1a7104508d3ebf27393ba0f2e81319.gif (245×180)" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I loved the language thing...it was awesome !! It was nice to see that even in a different language, Lahn still had quite the dirty mouth ;)<br><br><i>
  <strong>“You’re my gold, nahna xaxsah is my hahnee rah. Kay jahnan nahna lisa, na uvan tee luh kay. Ana kay jahnan nahna pahnsahna, Circe. Kay nayeesan tee. Fahzah.”</strong>
  <br>
  <br>
  <strong>“You’re my gold, your cunt is my liquid gold. I will have your mouth, you will give it to me. Then I will have your spirit, Circe. I will own it. Always.”</strong>
</i><br><br>KA writes some awesome Alpha men, but Lahn is the biggest and baddest Alpha out of all her books. He could be a extreme asshole and he seriously fucks up more than once !!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1489143555i/22188855.jpg" alt="a71793b71287569d7de0827db258d602.jpg (236×236): " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But no worries, because Circe is also the strongest and most wonderful heroine out of all KA's books. She is defnitely my all time favorite heroine ! She gave a lot, but she also tried to stayed true to herself and I really admired her for that.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1489143555i/22188856.jpg" alt="motherofdragons_upload_1397642258_300.jpg (300×300): " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b><i>“Then I whispered, “I love you, my Lahn,” and heard the swift hiss of his intake of breath. Then he buried his face in my neck and whispered back, “Loot kay hansahnalay na, my Circe.” And I love you, my Circe.”</i> </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1489143555ra/22188857.gif" alt="17201376.gif (500×261)" width="387" height="202" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So there you have it. My favorite KA book, my favorite hero and my favorite heroine !! Like I said...I have read this book many many times already and I am sure I will read it many times more !!</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2444467047" />
    <a title="NMmomof4" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/24665574-nmmomof4"><img alt="NMmomof4" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1515474309p2/24665574.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2444467047?book_show_action=true">Jul 03, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="NMmomof4" class="user" itemprop="url" name="NMmomof4" href="/user/show/24665574-nmmomof4">NMmomof4</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=contract-or-marriage-of-convenience">contract-or-marriage-of-convenience</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=neighbors-live-with">neighbors-live-with</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=not-safe">not-safe</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=unlikely-couple">unlikely-couple</a>,

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2444467047" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9824469959471326702"><b> 4 Stars <i>(Originally Read 7/3/2018)</i></b><br/><br/><b> 4.5 Stars <i>(Re-Read 1/14/2019)</i></b><br/><br/><b> 4.5 Stars <i>(Re-Read 11/12/2019)</i></b><br/><br/><b> 4.5 Stars <i>(Re-Read 5/21/2019)</i></b><br/><br/><b>Re-Read Update:</b> I'm not going to add much to this review after my re-read, because I still feel mostly the same about the book. I did enjoy it more (hence my increase in stars) and didn't have as many issues with the h as I did before. That could very well be because I remembered how everything works out and wasn't experiencing it for the first time. Still loved the H (an</span>
  <span id="freeText9824469959471326702" style="display:none"><b> 4 Stars <i>(Originally Read 7/3/2018)</i></b><br /><br /><b> 4.5 Stars <i>(Re-Read 1/14/2019)</i></b><br /><br /><b> 4.5 Stars <i>(Re-Read 11/12/2019)</i></b><br /><br /><b> 4.5 Stars <i>(Re-Read 5/21/2019)</i></b><br /><br /><b>Re-Read Update:</b> I'm not going to add much to this review after my re-read, because I still feel mostly the same about the book. I did enjoy it more (hence my increase in stars) and didn't have as many issues with the h as I did before. That could very well be because I remembered how everything works out and wasn't experiencing it for the first time. Still loved the H (and pictured him as Jason Momoa 😍), still loved how the h works through the language and culture barriers, and still simply loved the overall premise! I think this will go along with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11227040.Sweet_Dreams__Colorado_Mountain___2_" title="Sweet Dreams (Colorado Mountain, #2) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Sweet Dreams</a> as a book that I will turn to when I am looking for a good and reliable re-read.<br /><br /><b>2nd Re-Read Update:</b> Nothing really to add! Just a good, reliable re-read when I'm not feeling my tbr list 😘<br /><br /><b>3rd Re-Read Update:</b> Same as above, nothing much to add. I do wish the ending had more of their HEA though....<br /><br /><b>Overall Opinion: </b>This was an enjoyable read! I liked the whole alternate universe/everyone has a twin aspect going on! I'm not usually a fantasy or pnr fan, but if anyone has recommendations for books that are similar to this one -- please share! After reading such raving reviews I hesitantly started this one (hesitant because I was worried my expectations would let me down again), and I'm happy I read it! Definitely not KA's typical story, but enjoyable all the same. I liked the H, and I couldn't help but imagine him as Jason Momoa (like the hottie savage he is in Game of Thrones) 😉😉. I did, however, struggle with the h and her stubbornness at times. This also didn't have the epic epilogue that I come to expect from KA. I'm greedy, so I know that it's something I need to let go because I still would call it a HEA. I don't think this is "safe", because this has some scenes and aspects that many will struggle with (see Trigger spoiler tag below). Personally, I think in understanding that this is an alternate universe and with a completely different and primitive culture made it a little easier to accept those things. Overall this was a fun read, and I can see this being one I might re-read again down the road!<br /><br /><b>Brief Summary of the Storyline: </b> This is Circe and Lahn's story. Circe wakes up and finds herself in a cage with several other women that are telling her that she is part of the "wife hunt". She realizes quickly that she has no idea where she is or who these other people are. She then finds herself on the run while these huge, savage men chase after her and chain themselves to her neck. She ends up captured by the King of the strange land, and she is the new queen. After some rough first encounters, some huge language and cultural barriers, and some acceptance from Circe that this is her new reality -- she starts to adapt to her new life. Lahn is a fierce warrior to his people, but inside their home he is sweet and caring for Circe and they fall in love. There are some suspenseful moments, some sexy times, and some sweet scenes...and they get a HEA ending.<br /><br /><b>POV:</b> This was told in Circe's POV.<br /><br /><b>Overall Pace of Story: </b> Good. This is KA, so it's long! It even felt long at times, but I never skimmed and I thought it flowed well (it just was a lot that went on packed into the one book!).<br /><br /><b>Instalove:</b> No. BUT I think they move quickly and their circumstances definitely contribute to that, so it didn't feel insta to me.<br /><br /><b>H rating:</b> 4 stars. Lahn. I liked him. He made some big mistakes, but he was definitely a product of his upbringing because he didn't see the wrong in his actions at first. I loved how he cared for the h.<br /><br /><b>h rating:</b> 3 stars. Circe. She adapted pretty well considering it was some crazy circumstances, but I did feel like she was a little too stubborn at times though.<br /><br /><b>Sadness level: </b>Low/moderate. I cried a few times, but I never needed any tissues.<br /><br /><b>Push/Pull:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[There are a few instances of the h pushing the H away. The H is the main pursuer of the relationship.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Heat level:</b> Good. They have some good tension, chemistry, and scenes -- but not so much it takes away from the story.<br /><br /><b>Descriptive sex:</b> Yes<br /><br /><b>OW/OM drama:</b> No<br /><br /><b>Sex scene with OW or OM:</b> No <br /><br /><b>Cheating: </b> Kind of, but no specific details or descriptive scenes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ The h finds out that the warriors use slaves for sexual reasons as well as they bathe the warriors. She asks the H to stop using the slaves, and he agrees. It's never outright said that he had sexual relations with the slaves after he was married, but it kinda felt implied.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Separation:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[They are separated for ~5 months, but there was no mention or suggestion of other partners during this time.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Possible Triggers: </b>Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Rape (H rapes h at first), physical abuse (H hits the h once), and violence/slavery/suicide/murder (on page) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Closure: </b> This had pretty good closure with what I would call a HEA ending <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[they're married with babies <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. <br /><br /><b>Safety:</b> This one is probably <u>Not Safe</u> for most safety gang readers.<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />- <b>Does</b> have cheating (see above)<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have a descriptive sex scene with OW/OM<br />- <b> Does</b> have the h pushing the H away<br />- <b> Does</b> have a separation between the h and H<br />- <b> Does</b> have abuse<br />- <b>Does </b> have a HEA ending <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

<div id="review_776046181" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/776046181" />
    <a title="Lorena" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/24421069-lorena"><img alt="Lorena" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/776046181?book_show_action=true">Nov 28, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lorena" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lorena" href="/user/show/24421069-lorena">Lorena</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">NO ONE</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Lorena by: </span>
      Only myself to blame
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24421069-lorena?shelf=nope">nope</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24421069-lorena?shelf=kill-with-fire">kill-with-fire</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24421069-lorena?shelf=2013">2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24421069-lorena?shelf=rape-fantasy">rape-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24421069-lorena?shelf=tstl-heroine">tstl-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24421069-lorena?shelf=domineering-rage-beast">domineering-rage-beast</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer776046181" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13491034578044457133">Review contains strong themes including rape<br/><br/>The Golden Dynasty by Kristen Ashley is the story of Circe, a modern woman from Seattle, who wakes up in a parallel universe. She is upon waking subjected to a so called wife hunt, rape and forced into marriage. The story continues of the main characters' struggle to overcome their many differences and Circe’s struggle to accept this new world of the Korwahk and her new warrior husband Lahn.<br/><br/>I didn't like this book at all and <b>I especially loathe the her</b></span>
  <span id="freeText13491034578044457133" style="display:none">Review contains strong themes including rape<br /><br />The Golden Dynasty by Kristen Ashley is the story of Circe, a modern woman from Seattle, who wakes up in a parallel universe. She is upon waking subjected to a so called wife hunt, rape and forced into marriage. The story continues of the main characters' struggle to overcome their many differences and Circe’s struggle to accept this new world of the Korwahk and her new warrior husband Lahn.<br /><br />I didn't like this book at all and <b>I especially loathe the heroine’s acceptance of this world.</b> While there are numerous other things that irritated me in this book (such as the ridiculous made up language and the bad writing; punctuation errors, paragraphs overflowing with unnecessary adjectives, and all those inconsequential details that really don't make the world building any better) they really all pale in comparison.<br /><br />In order to create a depth of differences between the main characters, not only of language, but of morality, ethics and of a sense of right and wrong, the author created a fantasy world; <b>A misogynistic country dominated by chauvinistic, brutal men, a society in which masculinity and violence are emphasized and a culture in which rape and violence towards women are normalized.</b><br /><br />The world depicted in this book is made up of a brute horde of men who see it as their right to rape, abduct and abuse women. Women have no rights in their society, it is a warrior’s right to rape and claim a woman as his wife and treat her any way he likes, with no laws in place to prevent abuse. With this social order of dominant male warriors Kristen Ashley created the perfect psychological setting for these men to vent their hatred of women.<br /><br /><br /><u>The characters:</u><br />The female mc Circe is a modern woman. A modern woman, who was raised in equality to men, with rights, with freedom, with the choice to say no and above all, with a sense of right and wrong. But she strives to accept her new husband after he repeatedly rapes, beats and mistreats her and she strives to accept this misogynistic world of the Korwahk with "their way". Kristen Ashley created a weak, ignorant, materialistic, selfish and shallow character who doesn’t bother to look beyond her own bubble of relative safety. She doesn’t fight for all the women in the Korwahk society who suffer immeasurably, nor does she even try to free herself from her awful situation.<br /><br />As she becomes the new Korwahk queen, is given pretty jewelry and clothes, she surrounds herself with her circle of friends and screens herself off from the rest of the people. She sees only what she wants to; she calls her slaves “her girls”, gives them jewelry and clothes and overlooks the fact that they were brutally taken from their homes and forced to live out their lives as slaves, instead believing, that if she doesn’t treat them as slaves, it would make their lot in this world different. She really does not understand the concept of slavery and is actually baffled when one of her slaves betrayes her for her own people and her freedom (Teetru, the strongest, most likeable woman in this book as she actually fights against this society). <b>This kind of ignorance, born from looking the other way and being able to ignore the horror when it is not happening right in front of one's eyes, makes her such a weak and detestable woman.</b> She doesn’t give other women (the Horde's slaves who are forced into prostitution) who are kept as slaves a second thought, instead focusing on how it affects her and whether Lahn still as sex with them.<br /><br />She gets wrapped in this bubble by Lahn and is pampered as the Korwahk queen. She puts on her rose colored glasses and sits contently back surrounded by her friends, forgetting, ignoring or looking the other way (I never figured out which) as the rest of the women in this world continue to suffer. And she has seen what women are subjected to by their husbands! While she made a rather pointless attempt to help one woman, she never stopped to look at the bigger picture, never broke the silence and raised her voice against all the wrongness of this society, <b>never tried to change the way things are</b>, and never fought for justice and equality for women. <b>Instead, she focused on trying to accept her husband, his people and “their way”.</b><br /><br /><br />The male mc Lahn was born and raised into the Korwahk society and into the hierarchical command of the military with the power of weaponry exclusive to their hands, so it is of no surprise that he views horrific acts such as rape, abduction, slavery, forced marriage and violence against women to subdue, intimidate, punish and as a weapon as his right and as “their way”. If someone is raised to believe such values are fundamentally their right, how would one know of the wrongness of their acts? He is a brutal, cruel and ruthless warrior, who led his entire life as such, who takes what he wants regardless of the suffering of others. <b>But the reader is made to believe that such a man can change himself, his values, his belief in the warrior’s way and the way he thinks of the social mechanisms through which his society functions.</b> That he would come to view rape as an act of wrongness, after instrumenting it continuously as a weapon and as a way to control and subdue women, is just plain unbelievable.<br /><br />Not only this, but that such a man, a king to a horde of savages, would abandon the Korwahk warrior’s most crucial social instrument and their most horrible weapon of war – sexual violence against women – is extremely far-fetched. Especially after it is impressed upon Circe how crucial it is, that he as king must not be seen as weak or challenges would be issued.<br /><br /><b>That a person can change their entire being, their entire belief of what is right and wrong, in a matter of days is not only absurd but is a dangerous message to send.</b><br /><br /><br /><u>The romance:</u><br />First off, in my opinion, such a relationship never has a chance. Never mind the way he treats her, but there is literally a world of differences between the two and it's just not realistic that their relationship can ever work out. But that is beside the point, as this is about how the romance is depicted the book. <br />Their relationship progresses with no explanation and because of that, is not believable. Lahn falls in instant lust with her because she's the only blond woman. Then, after being raped continuously for three days, Circe one day just literally has an orgasm during another attack and she starts calling Lahn by pet names at the same time. This is the man who raped her for days! She doesn’t come to terms with her rape and is able to view her rapist as her new husband and lover in ONE day. It just continues this way; there is no believable romance between the main characters, Circe forgives Lahn for his mistreatment of her and romanticizes the times when he acts different towards her. The issue of the many differences between them is resolved by Lahn just changing his entire personality and way of thinking and Circe accepting everything just because “it is their way”.<br /><br /><br /><u>The society and "their way":</u><br />Seeing how this society is depicted in the book, the use of gender violence to control and subdue women becomes apparent. <b>In this social order depicted in the book, in which men as a social class are dominant over women and men are entitled to women’s bodies and their lives, the violence against women is one of the vital social mechanisms by which women are forced into a subordinate position.</b> Women in this society do not have any rights; they cannot speak up for themselves and have no legal way of seeking justice. Using a warrior’s weapon to defend themselves is an automatic death sentence. Those who are raised in this society are forced into subordinate positions; those who fight back against their oppressors are sentenced to death. The punishments for treason committed by women are sexual assault, violent rape, public humiliation and finally death. Women are kidnapped in raids and kept as slaves. <b>Gender violence is not random and not only about sex, but functions as a deliberate social function; asserting control over women’s' lives and keeping them second-class citizens.</b><br /><br />But all this doesn't matter to the female mc, for love is more important than such things as equality, freedom, justice and the right to choose.<br /><br />Gender violence is used to assert control over women of other countries as well: Raids and attacks on villages on the borders are committed as common occurrence. Sexual violence and rape of women are used as a weapon of war. While the heroine is horrified when she learns of these raids she only asks that Lahn not rape anyone - because then he would be cheating!<br />She is told - by a woman (Diandra, the most detestable character in this book as she conditions other women to accept “their way”) - that to prevent him from raping women during the raids she must fuck his brains out, because then Lahn wouldn't have the <b>need</b> to rape women! <br />First, <b>the use of rape in times of war is not a result of conflicts and not only about sex, but it is a pre-planned and deliberate military strategy and a weapon of war.</b> That he, as their leader, would agree not to rape anyone and thus not use one of their most devastating weapons of war is just not believable. Sexual violence is a weapon of war used to humiliate and terrify, to destroy societies and to eliminate cultural and religious traditions. Especially as it was pointed out in the book, that he as Korwahk King has to lead a strong example and not show weakness to avoid uprisings. <br />And second, <b>a woman is here conditioning another woman to assume the responsibility of a man's sexuality and of controlling his behavior</b>. I don't even have to point out how wrong it is, to make a woman assume such a responsibility.<br /><br />In addition to rape, girls and women of these attacked villages are abducted and forced into slavery. Women are kidnapped for the wife hunt and forced into marriages. Seen as spoils of war and as a warrior’s right, this just furthers to underline the belief of the Korvahk men that women are secondary to their world and as such to the world that matters.<br />But Circe accepts the use of rape as a weapon, the abduction and abuse of women, slavery and the overriding war culture as the new social norm because "it is their way".<br /><br /><br /><u>The depiction of misogyny:</u><br />The way that rape is depicted in this book is utterly sexist. The reader learns, that these warriors see it as their right to rape women and that they don’t view rape as an act of wrongness:<br /><blockquote>
  <i>he [Zahnin] kept using her [Sabine] body for the last three weeks as any warrior would feel his due from his wife. […] And <b>he didn’t understand it</b> but he’d been forcing her to live a nightmare for three weeks.</i>
</blockquote><br />But this is completely contradicted later on in the book, when we learn that they do indeed know the difference between consensual sex and rape. So, while they see nothing wrong with raping women, it’s an entirely different story when it’s a man being raped:<br /><blockquote>
  <i>“they don't allow homosexuality and they-?" Diandra shook her head. "No, Dax Lahn does, he does not seem to care. He <b>only punishes those who force it on others</b> who do not wish it”</i>
</blockquote><br />The way that male and female victims of rape are viewed differently, and the way that a rapist’s punishment depends on his victim's gender is <b>the most blatant portrayal of misogyny</b> in the book and <b>that I've ever seen in a romance book.</b><br /><br /><br /><u>The female mc's acceptance of "their way":</u><br />Now, the heroine struggled – understandably – to accept this society of prevailing warriors and their king Lahn. Her friend Diandra most adamantly insists that Circe must accept her new husband and their way, while the threat of violence hangs over her head should she not conform to her new social role. Diandra “helped” her accept her new place in this world by explaining that “it is their way”.<br /><b>The phrase “it is their way” is used throughout the book to explain and excuse these atrocious acts against humanity and to help the female mc accept this primitive, misogynistic land, its people, and their king.</b><br /><br />And so Circe changes a lot - not to the better - during the book and with her, her views on the way things are. <b>After three weeks, she</b> not only <b>accepts this society</b>, but also <b>sees nothing wrong anymore with "their way"</b>: In the beginning of the book she was naturally horrified by the way a warrior raped and abused his wife, Mahyah, and she even tried to help her. She also automatically hated that warrior because of the way he treated his wife. But then, later on in the book, Circe goes from sympathizing with a woman who was being badly abused by her husband to this:<br /><blockquote>
  <i>Then she [Sabine] got up and quickly backed away, her eyes glued in fear to Zahnin, her body shaking.<br />I studied her.<br />Yep, <b>this was why Zahnun was in such a bad mood</b>. Three weeks [of rape] and <b>she was still like this</b>?</i>
</blockquote><br />The woman was abducted and raped for three weeks and Circe is fucking worried about the rapist's fucking bad mood and is surprised that his victim "is still like this"? What the fuck!<br /><b>Circe goes from despising a man because of how he mistreats a woman to actually liking another man who rapes a woman for weeks. She goes from trying to help a woman escape from her rapist to actually "helping" another woman stay with her rapist!</b> And the reason, that after three weeks she has a completely different view on a rapist and his victim, is BECAUSE IT IS THEIR WAY.<br /><br /><br />All that violence against women happening in our world today BECAUSE IT IS THEIR WAY! There are too many societies in which such horrendous acts and worse are being committed, and it is also “their way”. This does not condone such acts. It does not make them all right. It most certainly does not serve as a way to justify them. And it definitely <b>does not mean that women have to accept them just because it is their way!</b><br /><br />Gender violence in this book is sanctioned in the name of tradition, because "it is their way". The way this society is set up and the way that Circe just accepts her subordinate place in it maintains the male dominance and female subjugation of this world and the violence against women is a manifestation of this unequal power relationship between men and women. <br /><br /><b>But instead of fighting against this status quo, Circe fights to accept it!</b><br /><br />And that is my biggest issue with the book: <b>That a modern woman could EVER accept these inexcusable and intolerable violations against humanity as the new social norm JUST because “it is their way”.</b><br /><blockquote>
  <i>"But as much as your world scared me, as much as your practices repulsed me, I still chose you."</i>
</blockquote><br />So, while countless women suffer and die every day because of the way things are in some parts of our world and while women continue to fight and die for not to having to accept the way things are in their societies, here we are, reading this <i>romance</i> book by Kristen Ashley, <b>in which a modern woman passively accepts her place in a misogynistic society where violence against women is normalized and tolerated in silence because it is "their way".</b><br /><br />While 300 girls were kidnapped in Nigeria earlier this year, sold into slavery and forced into marriages, here is this book by Kristen Ashley, in which the female mc is also kidnapped and forced into a marriage. She is told that she must accept everything as it is because "it is their way". And she fucking does! What kind of message does that send? Because, the Islamic extremists are also following their way. Does that condone or justify their horrendous acts? <b>NO!</b> <br /><br /><b>So why does “their way” condone and justify the <u>exact same</u> behavior in a romance book?</b><br /><br />I honestly can not understand all those five star ratings.<br /><br />I am guessing - and really hoping - that the author's only intention with this book, was to send the message that love conquers all differences. But dammit, don’t do it like this! <br />First of all, it’s just not realistic, and second, the way this acceptance in the name of love is depicted is just plain wrong and obscene. <b>Women (and men) should never, ever have to accept such a status quo just because it is "their way"!</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="13491034578044457133" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText12459335419739060681" style="display:none"><i> Reread #4848548469 on 4/21/18 </i><br />LOVE THIS BOOK<br /><br />So when I discovered one of my all time favorite books was released in paperback for the first time, I bought that paperback right away! I meant to skim my favorite parts, but ended up completely rereading the entire book. And it was just as good if not better the second time around.<br /><br />I am writing this review on a different edition of the book, so I think 2 reviews will show up and for that I am sorry if it bothers anyone. But since Goodreads doesn't have a reread option this was my only choice.<br /><br />Anyways this is one of those epic romances that completely tears you apart on the inside and then puts you back together again. It's unconventional and yet it's beautiful and quite possibly the best book this author has ever written. If you haven't read it yet, you need to.</span>

    <a title="Amy | Foxy Blogs" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs"><img alt="Amy | Foxy Blogs" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1366176904p2/9955253.jpg" /></a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Amy | Foxy Blogs" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amy | Foxy Blogs" href="/user/show/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs">Amy | Foxy Blogs</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/28593695-the-golden-dynasty">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs?shelf=2017-books">2017-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs?shelf=5-star-2017">5-star-2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs?shelf=april-2017">april-2017</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1971731989" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2361960054749649208">17 hours of audio bliss!!<b> My favorite Kristen Ashley book to date!!!</b><br/><br/>If you're a fan of<b> GAME OF THRONES</b> love story between Daenerys and Khal Drogo then this story is for you!!! This is how I pictured their love story had Khal Drogo stayed on the show longer. <br/><br/>READ IT!!! I'm already planning to re-read this book later this year!! <br/><br/><br/><b>SERIES</b><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12390650.Wildest_Dreams__Fantasyland___1_' title='Wildest Dreams (Fantasyland, #1) by Kristen Ashley' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1327913321s/12390650.jpg' alt='Wildest Dreams (Fantasyland, #1) by Kristen Ashley' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12458287.The_Golden_Dynasty__Fantasyland___2_' title='The Golden Dynasty (Fantasyland, #2) by Kristen Ashley' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1327913192s/12458287.jpg' alt='The Golden Dynasty (Fantasyland, #2) by Kristen Ashley' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13005310.Fantastical__Fantasyland___3_' title='Fantastical (Fantasyland, #3) by Kristen Ashley' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1327913381s/13005310.jpg' alt='Fantastical (Fantasyland, #3) by Kristen Ashley' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15817351.Broken_Dove__Fantasyland___4_' title='Broken Dove (Fantasyland, #4) by Kristen Ashley' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1385393334s/15817351.jpg' alt='Broken Dove (Fantasyland, #4) by Kristen Ashley' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17608224.Midnight_Soul__Fantasyland___5_' title='Midnight Soul (Fantasyland, #5) by Kristen Ashley' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1463680750s/17608224.jpg' alt='Midnight Soul (Fantasyland, #5) by Kristen Ashley' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/>The Fantasyland Series is a series of five novels that take place in our world and a parallel universe where fantasies are true... but perhaps no</span>
  <span id="freeText2361960054749649208" style="display:none">17 hours of audio bliss!!<b> My favorite Kristen Ashley book to date!!!</b><br><br>If you're a fan of<b> GAME OF THRONES</b> love story between Daenerys and Khal Drogo then this story is for you!!! This is how I pictured their love story had Khal Drogo stayed on the show longer. <br><br>READ IT!!! I'm already planning to re-read this book later this year!! <br><br><br><b>SERIES</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12390650.Wildest_Dreams__Fantasyland___1_" title="Wildest Dreams (Fantasyland, #1) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1327913321s/12390650.jpg" alt="Wildest Dreams (Fantasyland, #1) by Kristen Ashley" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12458287.The_Golden_Dynasty__Fantasyland___2_" title="The Golden Dynasty (Fantasyland, #2) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1327913192s/12458287.jpg" alt="The Golden Dynasty (Fantasyland, #2) by Kristen Ashley" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13005310.Fantastical__Fantasyland___3_" title="Fantastical (Fantasyland, #3) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_1023290345" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1023290345" />
    <a title="✰ Liz ✰ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27276528-liz"><img alt="✰ Liz ✰ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1451097545p2/27276528.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1023290345?book_show_action=true">Aug 10, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✰ Liz ✰ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="✰ Liz ✰ " href="/user/show/27276528-liz">✰ Liz ✰ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=dark-and-gritty">dark-and-gritty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=best-couples">best-couples</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=alpha-male-love">alpha-male-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=high-steam-alert">high-steam-alert</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1023290345" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3934705078959618980"><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1572891488ra/28401571.gif' width='' height='' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I know that many of my friends make fun of me for reading so many things at once but I just can't help it! While on vacation this past week, I couldn't help but pick up one of my faves! I absolutely adore this book. Circe and Lahn are two of my favorite characters of all time! This book has it all! Romance, passion, action, and the absolute best steamy scenes! It doesn't matter if you are a KA fan or not, this book is the best! Now I can start my next read with a big smile on my face! Everyone h</span>
  <span id="freeText3934705078959618980" style="display:none"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1572891488ra/28401571.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I know that many of my friends make fun of me for reading so many things at once but I just can't help it! While on vacation this past week, I couldn't help but pick up one of my faves! I absolutely adore this book. Circe and Lahn are two of my favorite characters of all time! This book has it all! Romance, passion, action, and the absolute best steamy scenes! It doesn't matter if you are a KA fan or not, this book is the best! Now I can start my next read with a big smile on my face! Everyone has their go-to book...this is mine! So glad I took the time to re-read one of my favorites!<br><br> <b>“You know I love you," I whispered in his ear.<br><br>"I know," he whispered back, turned, I pulled my arms away and he got on his knees in front of me, his hands framing my face.<br><br>I looked in his dark eyes.<br><br>"Do you know how much?" I kept whispering.<br><br>"How much, baby?" Lahn kept whispering too.<br><br>I bent my forehead to his and told him the truth. "More than my world.” </b><br><br> <b>Original read August 12, 2014</b><br>It's no surprise that I am a HUGE Kristen Ashley fan. I have enjoyed every single one of her books. There are not enough stars in the world to award to this book. The Golden Dynasty is raw, gritty, beautiful, action packed, and one of those books that stays with you. I feel it is necessary to warn readers that this book starts out very violent. Kristen Ashely wants to immerse us into this fantastical world. The only way to make that happen is to really put you there in that world. You have to feel every emotion of the heroine in order to grasp the depths of the love that Lahn and Circe find in each other. Now I will try to express in words just how much I adored every second of this read!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408252630i/10829904.jpg" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The story begins with Circe in a foreign realm. She went to sleep the night before in her apartment and has woken up in a cell full of scared women. She doesn't know what is happening but she is afraid and works quickly to assess her predicament. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408252630i/10829905._SY540_.jpg" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Circe quickly learns from another girl in the pen that she is about to participate in a ritual known as "the hunt". The women run and the warriors (aka savages) hunt, capture and then claim their bride. Circe gathers her strength and prepares to run for her life. (Obviously, she is far away from Seattle and just has to deal....love this girl)! <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408252630ra/10829906.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Somehow, the unbelievable happens. Circe has caught the eye of the mighty warrior King Lahn. He is known to watch the hunts and not participate. Yet Circe has caught his eye and he jumps into the hunt to claim her as his! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408252630ra/10829907.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Lahn catches Circe (after she has been traumatized by another warrior who tried to catch her first) and claims her. This claiming is not soft and sweet. It is rape. At this point, you might be checking the cover of the book. Is this a Kristen Ashley book? Is this a romance novel? What is actually happening here? <br><br>Circe is deeply traumatized by her new life. Yet she doesn't break down. She clings to her father's words of wisdom. She is an inspiration. <br><br><b>“What has been has been but what will be is what we make of it.” </b><br><br>Circe immerses herself in this new world. Although there is a language barrier, she tries to find kindness in her husband. Although he is rough and raw, we see moments of tenderness as he begins to show his adoration to his queen. Circe makes a friend who speaks her language. She begins to help guide her through the muddy waters of her new life. She also helps Circe understand Lahn. She serves as a translator and Lahn and Circe begin to communicate. <br><br><b>“He has bragged greatly about you. The Lahnahsahna, a true warrior’s wife. He told his people he did not claim you. He told his people he battled you before he won you. He told his people you challenged him. The warrior king’s bride fought like a warrior. She did not lay back and accept her fate. She stood strong and shouted in the face of a king. She fought and did not give up. Even knowing she’d taste defeat, she fought on, like a true warrior. He told his people you are not his queen. You are his warrior queen.” </b><br><br>Circe becomes a queen to her people. She begins to fall in love with her husband. She is such a strong heroine. She begins to fall deeply in love with Lahn. <br><br><b>“I was in love. Perhaps not with the man of my dreams, but with a man that was more man than any I’d ever encountered.” </b><br><br>Their love begins to grow. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408252630i/10829908.jpg" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>The road to happiness is filled with violence, miscommunication, and hurt. Yet this is a love story I will never forget. Bravo to Ms. Ashley for stepping WAY out of the box and creating such a masterpiece. If you aren't afraid to dig deep into an unbelievable world then look no further. This book has it all!!!!<br><br>💕<b>Re-read July 20-25, 2018</b>💕<br>This book will never get old. I love every second! <br><br>💕💕<b>Re-read July 1-4</b>💕💕<br><br>💕💕💕<b>Re-read July 20, 2020💕💕💕<br>This is an (F)BR with my girl SIMPLY NIK!!!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1595274500ra/29846802.gif" width="200" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1595274613ra/29846804.gif" width="200" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For more reviews/reveals/giveaways visit:<br><a href="https://craziesrusbookblog.wordpress.com//" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1588637625i/29416022.png" width="400" height="185" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450764696i/17467413.jpg" width="" height="50" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> <a href="https://twitter.com/CraziesRus" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450633462i/17450183.png" width="80" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> <a href="https://www.pinterest.com/craziesrus/" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450763751i/17467332.jpg" width="80" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> <a href="https://www.facebook.com/Crazies-R-Us-Book-Blog-171506803016307/timeline/" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450633462i/17450182.png" width="80" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </a><a href="https://plus.google.com/u/0/110273454171852792166/posts" rel="nofollow noopener"></a> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450764696i/17467413.jpg" width="" height="50" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="3934705078959618980" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1499198821?book_show_action=true">Jan 07, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~♡AB♡~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~♡AB♡~" href="/user/show/12180287-ab">~♡AB♡~</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1499198821" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1229346071600044103">★★★★★ <b>5 Stars</b> ★★★★★<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452687786i/17726420._SX540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>OK, mini review for this one.<br/><br/>I am so glad I read this! Dax Lahn = The Man<br/><br/>I hate fantasy crap, I don't like LoTR or Hobbits or (gasp) GoT! I don't mind a vamp and dabbled in shifters way back when Samantha Towle was writing them, but the thought of this series generally gave me the shivers so I steered well clear for years.<br/><br/>What a fucking idiot I am, because it turns out that this is now one of my favourite KA books ever! Really I should have been more open minded, I mean I love</span>
  <span id="freeText1229346071600044103" style="display:none">★★★★★ <b>5 Stars</b> ★★★★★<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452687786i/17726420._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>OK, mini review for this one.<br><br>I am so glad I read this! Dax Lahn = The Man<br><br>I hate fantasy crap, I don't like LoTR or Hobbits or (gasp) GoT! I don't mind a vamp and dabbled in shifters way back when Samantha Towle was writing them, but the thought of this series generally gave me the shivers so I steered well clear for years.<br><br>What a fucking idiot I am, because it turns out that this is now one of my favourite KA books ever! Really I should have been more open minded, I mean I love Outlander and that isn't 'real' either.<br><br>Basically, Circe is a normal kinda gal from Seattle who wakes up one day in another world which is very much like our world but from hundreds of years ago and maybe with some other oddities like talking tigers and magic. She finds herself as part of a 'wife hunt' whereby King Lahn sets his sights upon her and battles for her to be his queen.<br><br>I won't lie, the first part of their pairing is a bit brutal and savage, but it's fiction and rape and pillage doesn't bother me in a story if it's told well and redemption is key here. These men are savages but they are all so sweet deep down. This book is full of Alpha males, I was in heaven.<br><br>I loved both Lahn and Circe, they were fabulous and I loved it when they couldn't speak each others languages and had to communicate in other ways, it reminded me a bit of Transcendence by Shay Savage in that respect. Also, the sex scenes are some of, if not <i>the</i> best that Kristen Ashley has ever written. Hot and bothered doesn't describe my feelings adequately, it was like an inferno!<br><br>So all in all, I fell for my warrior Dax Lahn and his Golden Queen. Thank you to all of my ho's that recommended it to me. I am forever in your debt.<br><br><b>The Golden Dynasty is a standalone fantasy romance told in the heroine's POV. Also part of a series.</b><br> <br><div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1697581325" />
    <a title="Sophia Triad" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad"><img alt="Sophia Triad" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591419108p2/44642860.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1697581325?book_show_action=true">Jul 13, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sophia Triad" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sophia Triad" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad">Sophia Triad</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=dimensiontravel-paralleluniverse">dimensiontravel-paralleluniverse</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=4fantasy-lovestories">4fantasy-lovestories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>,

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1697581325" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13292323181827675875">I only have one word for this book: EPIC<br/>I have to say that it is the perfect example of how season 1 in Game of Thrones should have been developed, executed and concluded without breaking the hearts of Drogo's fans. <br/>Because trust me when I say that there is no chance someone who loves watching Game of Thrones and is reading the book for first time not picturing Dax Lahn as Drogo and Circe Quinn as Daenerys. <br/>In the downfalls of the book, I really missed the elves and the dragons from Fantasyland </span>
  <span id="freeText13292323181827675875" style="display:none">I only have one word for this book: EPIC<br />I have to say that it is the perfect example of how season 1 in Game of Thrones should have been developed, executed and concluded without breaking the hearts of Drogo's fans. <br />Because trust me when I say that there is no chance someone who loves watching Game of Thrones and is reading the book for first time not picturing Dax Lahn as Drogo and Circe Quinn as Daenerys. <br />In the downfalls of the book, I really missed the elves and the dragons from Fantasyland book 1 and the Korwahk language was a bit hard to get used to especially in the beginning of the book. Also although Circe was mentioned as a witch in the first book, I could not picture this fact in the second book until storms and rainbows have started making appearences in the sky.<br />But the last 100 pages of the book have seriously taken the story at a higher level and made me fall in love with the two main characters.<br />Lahn was purfect as the savage king who falls in love at first sight with beautiful golden Circe. <br />Circe was purfect as the innocent girl from Seattle who is taken unwillingly from her world, who is given no choice of her own life and who is repeatedly being raped before she forgives and falls in love.<br />Dortak was perfect as the man who was born to be hated.<br />I never expect to cry and have my heart that broken with a fantacy book...</span>

<div id="review_3195273840" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3195273840" />
    <a title="Starr (AKA Bam Bam) Rivers" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/74622641-starr-aka-bam-bam-rivers"><img alt="Starr (AKA Bam Bam) Rivers" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1581473939p2/74622641.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3195273840?book_show_action=true">Feb 18, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Starr (AKA Bam Bam) Rivers" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Starr (AKA Bam Bam) Rivers" href="/user/show/74622641-starr-aka-bam-bam-rivers">Starr (AKA Bam Bam) Rivers</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/28593695-the-golden-dynasty">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Starr (AKA Bam Bam) by: </span>
      ~*~Princess Nhya~*~
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/74622641-starr-aka-bam-bam-rivers?shelf=favorite-heroine">favorite-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/74622641-starr-aka-bam-bam-rivers?shelf=enemies-to-lovers">enemies-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/74622641-starr-aka-bam-bam-rivers?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/74622641-starr-aka-bam-bam-rivers?shelf=favorite-alpha-male">favorite-alpha-male</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3195273840" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3526311561457601786">I'm gonna try something new and write my review as I go along reading the book. I feel like this will be one of those books I have "revelations" about as I read along that won't be satisfied with just my stat updates. And also, it's a freaking LONG book! But I promised Princess N I'd read all of it and not skip so I will keep that promise IF SHE WILL DO THE SAME! (You know what I'm talking about P2)<br/><br/>Rating to come at the end. <br/><br/>So, impressions thus far are as follows:<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1582076304ra/28984853.gif' width='500' height='220' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Then:<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1582076304ra/28984852.gif' width='245' height='180' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Seriously, it's like readi</span>
  <span id="freeText3526311561457601786" style="display:none">I'm gonna try something new and write my review as I go along reading the book. I feel like this will be one of those books I have "revelations" about as I read along that won't be satisfied with just my stat updates. And also, it's a freaking LONG book! But I promised Princess N I'd read all of it and not skip so I will keep that promise IF SHE WILL DO THE SAME! (You know what I'm talking about P2)<br><br>Rating to come at the end. <br><br>So, impressions thus far are as follows:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1582076304ra/28984853.gif" width="500" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Then:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1582076304ra/28984852.gif" width="245" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Seriously, it's like reading the romance version of Kahl Drago and Daenerys from The Game of Thrones by Martin. Here are the similarities:<br><br>* warrior clan speaking their own language, savage, big dark haired, dark skinned men. Think Cavemen on horses.<br>* Heroine is fair skinned, fair haired, wedded by force (he "claimed" her) and raped 7 times before the sex was sorta consensual<br>* they speak diff languages so they don't understand each other. It's the age old language between men and women that's spoken here - grunts, facial expressions, touches, sex.<br>* There's a white animal pet. Tho here it's a baby tiger, it's named Ghost. In GoT, Ghost is the name of the MC Hero's wolf. <br>* Blondie is the long-prophesied queen of whatever<br>* He's BIG (6'7" or some such), she's tiny (barely over 5 feet)<br><br>Lots of differences, obviously, this being a romance with the h being plucked out of modern day Seattle (she's an office manager!) and waking up in this fantasy world in the middle of a bride hunt. <br><br>But still, my bet is that this book was inspired by the GoT and not the other way around. Hey, nothing against it, all authors are inspired by something, and if it's not out right plagiarism, do what you gotta do.<br><br>I do admit to being disappointed in GoT that Drago and D never got their HEA. How that warrior met his end was just so sad. But then, there are no such things as HEA in GoT so that wasn't surprising. <br><br>It's good to be looking forward to that HEA for Lahn and Circe here. So.<br><br>So far so good.<br><br><b> Alright. So here's my review, finally finished this LONG ass book!<br><br>All of Ashley's stuff is long. I think there's only 1 book I've read &lt; 500 pages. I have the same complaint I always have: it doesn't have to take so many pages!!<br><br>Thankfully, about 85% of this one was worth reading every word. And yes, I read all the other 15% too, bc SOMEONE made me.<br><br>Look, I loved it. Full stop.<br><br>I love Lahn and Circe is pretty adorable herself. There were a few errors in the book, but I didn't bother to highlight them. I was in a hurry to read the story.<br><br>As I note below, you have to suspend belief. Not just because this is fantasyland, but emotional belief. A modern woman with modern sensibilities, morals, and who's loved and pampered by a very good man (her father), is thrust into a strange world with big dark warriors who hunt brides, then consummate the deal with a raping... well, you'd think there'd be some emotional trauma involved.<br><br>Nope, none. Not even after the first time. And not after the first 7 times. Tho Circe sure did warm up to her gorgeous husband when he treated her well by being gentle. Guess being attracted to your rapist help with the falling in love thing.<br><br>It's a pretty big leap to make for anyone's brain.<br><br>But, this is fantasy romance and what other choice does a strong woman have but to suck it up and make the best out of a rotten situation.<br><br>But hey, at least her husband is the biggest, baddest, most gorgeous warrior king in the land and can give her multiple orgasms multiple times a day.<br><br>All's well that ends well.<br><br>I can't give this 5 stars bc ultimately, I'm not sure I'm rereading this book. Firstly, it's LONG, so it's not like a quick treat some lonely night. Secondly, well...<br><br>KA's characters seem to blend into each other. I love most of them, don't get me wrong. I especially like the men in her books. All alpha males who have a very soft spot for their women. Who don't hesitate to sleep around when it's not THE ONE, as alpha males are expected to do, I suppose. They tend to not talk much, unless they have something important to say. And tho they might not say it, they are very observant and sensitive. They CARE.<br><br>Great men.<br><br>She writes mostly great heroines too. Circe is no different.<br><br>It's just they all blend together. The interactions. The lengthiness. Replace the time, place and plot, and you have fundamentally similar characters. Which is probably why I gave a couple of her other books 5 stars, because they were more "new to me" at the time.<br><br>Now I'm kinda used to it. And tho I like this couple and story quite a lot, I'm not sure at this point that it's "unique" enough to get 5 stars.<br><br>Still, I do like the book. And there's at one point when Lahn finally breaks down in the end and expresses his defeat after 8 months of trying to win Circe back that I got a little teary. <br><br>Otherwise, this book didn't provoke as strong reactions in me as some other books. I like to be provoked.<br><br>Thanks to Princess Nhya for recommending it!</b><br><br>All right, I upgraded the rating to 5 stars... mainly bc of Dax Lahn... The scene with "mine"..."yours" and when he said he hadn't had a woman in 8 months... those scenes cinched it for me :)</span>
  <a data-text-id="3526311561457601786" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer6841805968730280629">Dax Lahn screamed of Drogo from the Games of Thrones and picturing him looking like Jason Mamoa was no hardship. I absolutely loved his character. There is nothing better than a dominant alpha who turns into such a protective loving mate to his woman. Even with the beginning of this story having some scenes that I would normally abhor in my romance novel, the author did such a good job of explaining it that I couldn't even hold their customs against them. That being said, there are triggers in t</span>
  <span id="freeText6841805968730280629" style="display:none">Dax Lahn screamed of Drogo from the Games of Thrones and picturing him looking like Jason Mamoa was no hardship. I absolutely loved his character. There is nothing better than a dominant alpha who turns into such a protective loving mate to his woman. Even with the beginning of this story having some scenes that I would normally abhor in my romance novel, the author did such a good job of explaining it that I couldn't even hold their customs against them. That being said, there are triggers in this book. For a heroine, Circe was one of the best I've read so far. These two as a couple were what I like to read in my MC's. The author could have continued this story into 10 more books and I don't think I would ever get bored of hearing about them or their world. This book deserves more than 5 Stars!</span>
