              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=pn-romance">pn-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1341118234" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2527188410410923322"><blockquote>
  <b>⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱*Still Quite Enjoyable*⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱</b>
</blockquote> <br/><b>
  <u>Second re-read: 04.09.2019</u>
</b><br/>I decided to re-read this one again as I remember liking the story about <b>Dahksahna Circe</b>, the golden warrior queen and <b>King/Dax Lahn</b> of Korwahk nation. The parallelunivers is a awesome concept that is an absolute joy to read about, though it can be a bit confusing at time. One thing I noticed this time around, was how annoyed I because at Circe calling Lahn ‘baby’ all the time. There was also the difficult to understand what t</span>
  <span id="freeText2527188410410923322" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱*Still Quite Enjoyable*⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱</b>
</blockquote> <br><b>
  <u>Second re-read: 04.09.2019</u>
</b><br>I decided to re-read this one again as I remember liking the story about <b>Dahksahna Circe</b>, the golden warrior queen and <b>King/Dax Lahn</b> of Korwahk nation. The parallelunivers is a awesome concept that is an absolute joy to read about, though it can be a bit confusing at time. One thing I noticed this time around, was how annoyed I because at Circe calling Lahn ‘baby’ all the time. There was also the difficult to understand what the hell the Korwahk was talking about, even after Circe learned their language. Strange as I cannot remember the latter being a problem before. That being said, I like the characters; the male characters are hot alpha male, and in this case terrific warriors. <br><br><b>
  <i>Kristen Ashley</i>
</b> has that <b>great talent with writing amazing alpha males</b>, whilst for me, her female characters always annoys the living shit out of me. A while Circe can be a bit annoying, she's by far one of my favorite female characters of KA, if not <i>the</i> favorite, because there's little that do annoy me with her. She's sweet, kind, but also fierce. <b>Overall, I'm glad I re-read it again</b>, I still enjoyed it very much and I didn't skim (though I have to be honest, there was some points where I felt myself <i>starting</i> to skim but went back and read it properly). Maybe I should re-read more from this series...<br><b>New Rating</b>: 3.5 stars.<br><br><b><u>Other Characters</u>:</b><br>→ <b>Seerim</b>, a warrior of The Horde, his wife <b>Diandra</b>. She teaches Circe the new world she has ended up in. Their daughter, <b>Sheena</b> (12).<br>→ <b>Dortak</b>, a creepy warrior of The Horde who wants the throne.<br>→ <b>Teetru</b>, the boss of sorts (of the slaves), <b>Jacanda</b>, <b>Packa</b>, <b>Gaal</b> and <b>Beetus</b>, Circe's ‘slaves’, a gift from Lahn. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Teetru became a traitor to Circe for her people, the Maroo. Lahn killed her. Circe get's a new slave; <b>Quixa</b>, she was older than Jacanda and Beetus, younger than Gaal and Packa and she was Korwahk, and Jacanda, became the new leader of the girls after they lost Teetru. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>→ <b>Geoffrey</b>, a man from Middleland. Middleland is ruled by King <b>Baldur</b>, who is a greedy, cruel man. <br>→ <b>Karrim ‘The Eunuch’</b>, he's the charge of the scouts who search for the wives for the Hunt, of the Hunt and its celebrations, of the warrior selections and once the warriors are selected, he chooses who will be trained by whom then, once they are of an age, who will be assigned to whom. He was cast out for being gay (?) by the previous Dax, but when Lahn became the Dax he tracked him down and gave him the job.<br>→ <b>Narinda</b>, a woman who became a bride in the Hunt and help Circe understand what was going on. <b>Feetak</b>, her husband.<br>→ <b>Nahka</b>, a bride of the warrior <b>Bohtan</b>, who's son Circe saved when the boy was choking.<br>→ <b>Bain</b> and <b>Zahnin</b>, two of Circe's personal guards. <b>Oahsee</b>, Bain's wife. <b>Sabine,</b> Zahnin's wife. Zahnin is Lahn's closest lieutenant.<br>→ <b>Claudine</b>, a friend of Diandra who knows French, and helped teach Sabine Korwahk.<br>→ <b>Char</b> and <b>Vuntus</b>, Nahka’s two BFFs. Their husbands, <b>Tark</b> and <b>Yoonan</b>.<br>→ <b>Twinka</b>, Lahn's house slave who looked after his residence in Korwahn while he was away.<br>→ <b>Harold Quinn</b>, Circe's father.<br>→ <b>Marlene</b>, Circe's best friend in Seattle. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I didn’t know where I was or how I got there. I wasn’t certain what was happening. I went to bed in my bed in a world I understood and I woke up here in a world that was entirely foreign to me, everything about it, and not one thing about it was good.<br>And now I was running for my life.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445268775i/16623124.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>Re-read: 10.10.2016</u>
</b><br><b>Still fantastic:</b> I love this book. I think I might even love it more than the first book, though I'm not so sure who I love the most <b>Frey Drakkar</b> (<i>
  <b>Wildest Dreams</b>
</i>) or <b>Dax (King) Lahn</b>... They are both amazing, hot and alpha male. So I'll just go for both. <b>Circe Kaye Quinn</b> (35) is, too, a great character, who doesn't make me annoyed, which is actually rare these days... Second time reading the book and it's still so damn good. I'm 120% sure I'll be re-reading this one again, and book one. Kristen Ashley do know how to write terrific books, I must say...<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“What has been has been but what will be is what we make of it.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b><u>Quick basic facts</u>:</b><br><b>Genre</b>: - (Adult) Fantasy Romance (M/F).<br><b>Series</b>: - Series (Can Be Read As A Standalone), Book Two. <br><b>Love triangle?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Cheating?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Unsure. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>HEA?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Favorite character?</b> - Dax Lahn.<br><b>Would I read more by this author/or of series?</b> - Yes.<br><b>Would I recommend this book/series?</b> - Yes.<br><b>Will I read this again in the future?</b> - Probably.<br><b>Rating</b> - 4 Stars.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445268775i/16623124.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b><u>First read review</u>:</b><br>Simply said, I <b>loved</b> it! Thank you so much, V, for reminding (recommend it to me again) me of this book! I'm sure that if it weren't for you saying I would love it, then I wouldn't have read it at all ;P<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437589820ra/15600455.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437589820ra/15600456.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437589820ra/15600457.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437589821ra/15600458.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437589821ra/15600459.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437589821ra/15600460.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437589821ra/15600461.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437589821ra/15600462.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer797244674" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8774361205476928546"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387894878i/7693821._SX540_.jpg' width='385' height='480' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>It’s a known fact that I don’t read synopses and loving Wildest Dreams had me expecting more sleigh rides, castles and fancy parties. What I got was <b>BRUTAL </b>but nonetheless <b>FANTASTIC</b>.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1491898355ra/22458526.gif' width='350' height='325' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This story opens in one hell of a horrific situation and I was longing for a card game in the pub like in the first book of this series. <br/><br/>Kristen Ashley brought a brutal, savage, warrior king (the most alpha male she has ever written) to fall in love despite language, culture and world barriers was truly mesmerizing. </span>
  <span id="freeText8774361205476928546" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387894878i/7693821._SX540_.jpg" width="385" height="480" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It’s a known fact that I don’t read synopses and loving Wildest Dreams had me expecting more sleigh rides, castles and fancy parties. What I got was <b>BRUTAL </b>but nonetheless <b>FANTASTIC</b>.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1491898355ra/22458526.gif" width="350" height="325" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This story opens in one hell of a horrific situation and I was longing for a card game in the pub like in the first book of this series. <br><br>Kristen Ashley brought a brutal, savage, warrior king (the most alpha male she has ever written) to fall in love despite language, culture and world barriers was truly mesmerizing. I may be in the minority, but I thought there was no way in hell that I would want to stay with these barbaric people, but Kristen Ashley changed my mind.<br><br><b>
  <i>“He has decided he likes the meaning of honey best but he prefers how you speak when you call him baby. He is, of course, a ‘big guy’ and simply finds it amusing you would point this out.”</i>
</b><br><br>Despite all the barriers this couple <b>KICKED ASS</b> and stole my heart. <br><br>As for quotes, here’s just a few…<br><br><b>
  <i>”It started as a nightmare but now seems like the sweetest dream.”</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>”I gave up my world for you.”</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>”I couldn’t dream a better you.”</i>
</b><br><br>What a rollercoaster of emotions I experienced during this book! I winced, cried and swooned. <br><br><b>KRISTEN ASHLEY YOU ARE MY QUEEN!</b> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/663146.gif" width="350" height="325" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br></span>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3716081-it-s-just-me-shelly-b?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer551155932" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2881672984574643002"><b>“He is a savage. Tales of his exploits have spread wide. Very cruel. Heartless.”</b><br/><br/>King Lahn or Dax Lahn if you speak Korwahk<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411908i/809715._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>He is a savage and me likey savages!!!!!!!! He was so perfect in every primitive way possible!! The people that he ruled, the Korwahk nation are basically savages, the warriors pick their brides in a hunt.<br/><br/>Yes people a hunt!! All the beauties of many nations are basically kidnapped and the warriors, of this race of people, get to pick their bride but then they have to hunt the</span>
  <span id="freeText2881672984574643002" style="display:none"><b>“He is a savage. Tales of his exploits have spread wide. Very cruel. Heartless.”</b><br><br>King Lahn or Dax Lahn if you speak Korwahk<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411908i/809715._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He is a savage and me likey savages!!!!!!!! He was so perfect in every primitive way possible!! The people that he ruled, the Korwahk nation are basically savages, the warriors pick their brides in a hunt.<br><br>Yes people a hunt!! All the beauties of many nations are basically kidnapped and the warriors, of this race of people, get to pick their bride but then they have to hunt them and battle for the rights for her. If you lose well tough shit, you should of fought harder!<br><br>It's crazy....but CRAZY GOOD!!!!!!<br><br>Like crazy good I would like to be in the hunt...I mean these warriors fighting for you.....<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411908ra/809716.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Of course Dax Lahn, or King Lahn, won his prize because he is BADASS!!!! OMG I cant even explain it properly......he's just that good!! <br><br>Now he has his bride...his Queen...Circe. She's the Golden Queen...his Tigress. However, Lahn didn't get a submissive female from his world. <br><br>Oh no no no.....Circe comes from our world. He just doesn't understand this woman telling what to do but he REALLY really likes his little tigress!!! Or as he would say, "Kah Lahnahsahna." So he's trying and bless his savage heart he does try!!!!<br><br>Circe has now become one of my all time fav female book characters. She was great, I loved her character because she was intimidated by Lahn but at the same time she wasn't...she stayed true to herself through out and gave a few concessions but so did he, so that was understandable.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411908ra/809717.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>These two are fabulous together!!!! This book takes you through a lot of ups and downs with them but it's so worth it!!!<br><br><br>This books was crazy, gruesome at times, beautiful, it was literally a little of everything and... I loved IT!!!!!!!!!!!!<br><br>Sometimes with books I REALLY love I don't know how to express how great they are and this is one them!!! Honestly I'm not a huge KA fan but this book to me is fantastic......these characters will remain with me for a long time!!!<br><br><br><br><b>buddy read with Vishous and Blacky:))))))</b><br><br></span>

  <span id="freeText12223201975809916773" style="display:none">F##k me Pink.... what a rollercoaster of a ride. Swore I would never read it - it is Fantasy - HATE Fantasy, hate vampires, hate time travel books - but it is KA so after I saw some of my GR buddies had given it great ratings decided to dive in - Thanks H.J. for the lend but I will probably end up getting my own copy. Freaking awesome - totally got into their world - it was so believable - Lahn - Hunt me down anytime Babe! Felt a bit for poor Pop at the end but as long as his girl was happy he was. I am still on a high after reading it .... Off to watch Homeland now so maybe that will sober me up a bit. Thanks for all the positive reviews - if it wasn't for you I probably would not have read it. Saying that I am never going to read Twilight and all that stuff..... What to read next, that is the question. Excuse the language at the beginning of the review but being Irish I think I am allowed to use the "F" word to express myself.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398015i/768716._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380761012i/3120719.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380761012i/3120720.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('4fnvBVmWuEJD8mgDUJJ3ey4Ir0CI/K7zJ97xJeHz4HQwy34kTIbVNlxKoHi59lzJwNAns8HLhrt/YTCab0Yk4A==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('4fzsHo+7//I/NVWFrl+2/X3V83B6oxyFrwSK1DfH20gwzn0/mquShiCNnf5HO51Pkw17gzOUNM33u0truXIf3A==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

  <span id="freeText12962731582923606234" style="display:none">Kristen Ashley was born in Gary, Indiana, USA. She nearly killed her mother and herself making it into the world, seeing as she had the umbilical cord wrapped around her neck (already attempting to accessorise and she hadn't taken her first breath!). <br /><br />Kristen grew up in Brownsburg, Indiana but has lived in Denver, Colorado and the West Country of England. Thus she has been blessed to have friends and family around the globe. Her posse is loopy (to say the least) but loopy is good when you want to write.<br /><br />Kristen was raised in a house with a large and multi-generational family. They lived on a very small farm in a small town in the heartland and existed amongst the strains of Glenn Miller, The Everly Brothers, REO Speedwagon and Whitesnake (and the wardrobes that matched).<br /><br />Needless to say, growing up in a house full of music, clothes and love was a good way to grow up. <br /><br />And as she keeps growing up, it keeps getting better.</span>

      <div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/work/quotes/17441876-the-golden-dynasty">Quotes from The Golden Dynasty</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;I could not dream a better you.” <br /><br />Oh my God. <br /><br />Oh… my… God. <br /><br />Did he just say that? <br /><br />I stared into his warm eyes. <br /><br />He just said that. <br /><br />And that was so sweet, so unexpected but so welcome, my breath arrested and all I could do was continue staring at him. <br /><br />He wasn’t done. “A better wife, a better queen. Not even in a dream could I create better than you.&rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>
              &mdash;
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/quotes/607374-i-could-not-dream-a-better-you-oh-my-god">141 likes</a>
            </nobr>
            <div class="clear"></div>
          </div>
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;<i> "I gave up a world for you." <br /> He glared at me, not giving me anything.<br /> I kept right on going. "I thought, perhaps, when I learned I had powers, I might be able to use them to go home," his eyes flashed but that was all I got so I kept on going, "but not for good. My father isn't dead." Another flash. "He's alive and at home and living maybe with a fake Circe. He'll know the difference, though, I KNOW it. He's out of his mind with worry, I know that too. He's wondering where I am and if I'm okay and how to get me back. I also know that. I know that and I know that my life was good. I loved my life. I loved my home. I loved my job. I had a lot of people who loved me that loved me back." I sucked in a breath and then whispered, "But as much as your world scared me, as much as our practices repulsed me, I still chose you."<br /> His torso jerked, it was almost imperceptible, but I caught it.<br /> I kept at him. "I gave up my world for you, Lahn. I sat at your side through things people in my world would find loathsome and I did it with my head held high. I even felt 'pride' that I could endure, that I could be a good queen to you.......Everything I did in this fucking place, even before I fell in love with you, was for...fucking...YOU." <i></i></i>&rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>
              &mdash;
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/quotes/605545-i-gave-up-a-world-for-you-he-glared">92 likes</a>
            </nobr>
            <div class="clear"></div>
          </div>
